#Use this when the parliament is enabled
azkare_parliament_setup = {
	hidden_effect = {
		4500 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = azkare_parliament_calculations_pulse }
		arkare_parliament_variables = {		#this one the one below are province groups
			set_variable = { which = azkareRepresentationChange value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareAutonomyPerRepresentation value = 0.5 }
		}
		arkare_parliament_culture_group_variables = {
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRepChange value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareNbRepCulture value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareNbUnrepCulture value = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = azkareNbLegionBonuses value = 0 }
	}
}

azkare_parliament_change_autonomy_per_rep_effect = {	#Required arguments: amount = x
	arkare_parliament_variables = { change_variable = { which = azkareAutonomyPerRepresentation value = $amount$ } }
}

#-------------------# Calculations #------------------------#

azkare_parliament_calculations = {
	azkare_parliament_representation_calculations = yes
	azkare_parliament_country_effects = yes
	azkare_parliament_province_effects = yes
	azkare_parliament_update_capital_names = yes
}

azkare_parliament_representation_calculations = {
	#Variables are stored in provinces, which are themselves contained in the 'arkare_parliament_variables' province group (one province per culture)
	arkare_parliament_variables = {
		set_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 0 }
	}
	
	#The provinces below contain the variables for culture groups
	arkare_parliament_culture_group_variables = {
		set_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 0 }
	}
	
	every_owned_province = {
		export_to_variable = { which = dev value = development }
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = culture
			#Bom Culture Group (culture group variables stored in the 4565 province)
			ranilau = {
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			chengrong = {
				4600 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			risbeko = {
				4572 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			biengdi = {
				4580 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			teplin = {
				4941 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}
				4565 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }
					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			gon = {
				4771 = {

					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}
				}

					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }
					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = dev }
						change_variable = { which = azkareGroupNbSeats value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}

			phonan = {
				5429 = {
					set_variable = { which = dev which = PREV }

					if = { limit = { PREV = { has_seat_in_parliament = yes } }
						change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = dev }
					}

					change_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev which = dev }

	arkare_parliament_variables = {		# Province groups that contains all the provinces that store the azkareCultureDev and azkareRepresentation variables
		limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev value = 1 } }
		divide_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareCultureDev }
		multiply_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 100 }
		change_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareRepresentationChange }	# representation changes due to scripted effects uses
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 100 } }
			set_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 100 }
		}
	}
	
	arkare_parliament_culture_group_variables = {
		limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareCultureGroupDev value = 1 } }
		divide_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation which = azkareCultureGroupDev }
		divide_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation value = 10 }		#to make the numbers after the coma disappear
		multiply_variable = { which = azkareGroupRepresentation value = 1000 }
	}

	
	# Most Represented Culture Calculations
	
	REB = { set_variable = { which = azkareNbRepCulture value = 0 } }
	
	4565 = {
		save_event_target_as = azkare_most_represented_culture
		set_variable = { which = azkareNbRepCulture value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = azkareNbUnrepCulture value = 0 }
		azkare_parliament_bom_variables = {
			clr_province_flag = azkare_most_represented
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = event_target:azkare_most_represented_culture } }
				save_event_target_as = azkare_most_represented_culture
			}
		}
		
		event_target:azkare_most_represented_culture = { set_province_flag = azkare_most_represented }
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:azkare_most_represented_culture = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 100 } } }
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep value = 70 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep value = 60 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep value = 40 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:azkare_most_represented_culture = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 80 } } }
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep value = 50 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep value = 40 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep value = 30 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:azkare_most_represented_culture = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation value = 60 } } }
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep value = 30 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep value = 20 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep value = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep value = 20 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep value = 10 }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep which = azkareAcceptableRepChange }
		change_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep which = azkareAcceptableRepChange }
		change_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep which = azkareAcceptableRepChange }
		
		azkare_parliament_bom_variables = {
			set_variable = { which = azkareAcceptableRep which = PREV }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMinorlyUnrep which = PREV }
			set_variable = { which = azkareMajorlyUnrep which = PREV }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareAcceptableRep } }
				PREV = { change_variable = { which = azkareNbRepCulture value = 1 } }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = azkareNbRepCulture value = 1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareCultureDev value = 0.01 } }
				PREV = { change_variable = { which = azkareNbUnrepCulture value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}

		if = { limit = { has_province_flag = azkare_most_represented check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareAcceptableRep } }

azkare_parliament_local_representation_effect = {
	
	# Local min autonomy
	
	$culture_province$ = {
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 1 } }
			if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 5 } } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 10 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_5 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 15 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_10 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 20 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_15 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 25 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_20 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 30 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_25 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 35 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_30 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 40 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_35 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 45 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_40 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 50 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_45 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 55 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_50 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 60 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_55 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 65 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_60 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 70 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_65 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 75 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_70 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 80 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_75 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 85 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_80 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 90 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_85 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 95 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_90 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareLocalAutonomy value = 100 } } }
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_95 duration = -1 } }
			}
			else = {
				PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_seats_autonomy_100 duration = -1 } }
			}
		}
		
		
		# Unrepresented Maluses
		
		if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareMajorlyUnrep } } }
			PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_unrepresented_culture duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareMinorlyUnrep } } }
			PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_majorly_unrepresented_culture duration = -1 } }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkareRepresentation which = azkareAcceptableRep } } }
			PREV = { add_province_modifier = { name = azkare_parliament_minorly_unrepresented_culture duration = -1 } }
		}
	}
}

azkare_parliament_legions_calculations = {
	set_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses which = azkareNbCultureRepresented }
	set_variable = { which = azkareLegionInfantryCostBonus which = azkareNbCultureRepresented }
	set_variable = { which = azkareLegionForcelimitBonus which = azkareNbCultureRepresented }
	divide_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses value = 10000 }
	multiply_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses value = 1000 }
	subtract_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses which = azkareNbLegionBonuses }
	if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses value = 0 } } }
		set_variable = { which = azkarePossibleLegionBonuses value = 0 }
	}
